#Balloon names for different cultures/countries
curtiss_balloon_type = { #From top to bottom decides which name list is appropriate. E.g. is a country with French as primary culture --> French names
	type = country
	
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				country_has_primary_culture = cu:alemannic
				AND = {
					exists = c:SWI
					c:SWI = root
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_swiss_balloon_name #The localization key references the next custom localization list further down.
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				country_has_primary_culture = cu:french
				AND = {
					exists = c:FRA
					c:FRA = root
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_french_balloon_name
	}

	text = {

					exists = c:OCC

			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_occitan_balloon_name
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				country_has_primary_culture = cu:breton
				AND = {
					this ?= c:BRI
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_breton_balloon_name
	}

	text = {

curtiss_custom_generic_balloon_name = {
	type = country

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:curtiss_balloon_name_randomizer_var = 1
		}
		localization_key = custom_balloon_name_endurance
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:curtiss_balloon_name_randomizer_var = 2
		}
		localization_key = custom_balloon_name_windweavers_enigma

	text = {

			var:curtiss_balloon_name_randomizer_var = 3

	text = {

		localization_key = custom_balloon_name_celestial_sojourner

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:curtiss_balloon_name_randomizer_var = 5
		}
		localization_key = custom_balloon_name_empyrean_endeavor
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {

		}
		localization_key = custom_balloon_name_daedalus_dream

#########Balloonist Altitude Flights##############################################################

curtiss_balloonist_altitude_flight_type = {
	type = country
	random_valid = yes
	
	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:new_balloon_altitude_var < 5000
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_altitude_under_5000_custom_1
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:new_balloon_altitude_var >= 5000
			var:new_balloon_altitude_var < 9000
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_altitude_under_9000_custom_1
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:new_balloon_altitude_var >= 9000
			var:new_balloon_altitude_var < 12000
			NOT = {
				has_technology_researched = watertube_boiler
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_altitude_under_12000_no_tools_custom_1
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:new_balloon_altitude_var >= 9000
			var:new_balloon_altitude_var < 12000
			has_technology_researched = watertube_boiler
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_altitude_under_12000_tools_custom_1
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:new_balloon_altitude_var >= 12000
			var:new_balloon_altitude_var < 16000
			NOT = {
				has_technology_researched = watertube_boiler
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_altitude_under_16000_no_tools_custom_1
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:new_balloon_altitude_var >= 12000
			var:new_balloon_altitude_var < 16000
			has_technology_researched = watertube_boiler
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_altitude_under_16000_tools_custom_1
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:new_balloon_altitude_var >= 16000
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_altitude_over_16000_custom_1
	}
}



#########Balloonist Distance Flights##############################################################

#title
curtiss_balloonist_distance_flight_title_type = {
	type = country
	random_valid = yes
	
	text = {
		trigger = {
			curtiss_distance_record_country_broken_trigger = no
			curtiss_time_record_country_broken_trigger = no
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_distance_title_no_record
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			curtiss_distance_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
			curtiss_time_record_country_broken_trigger = no
			curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = no
			curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = no
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_distance_title_distance_record_country
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			curtiss_distance_record_country_broken_trigger = no
			curtiss_time_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
			curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = no
			curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = no
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_distance_title_time_record_country
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			curtiss_distance_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
			curtiss_time_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
			curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = no
			curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = no
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_distance_title_both_records_country
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
			curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = no
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_distance_title_distance_record_global
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = no
			curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_distance_title_time_record_global
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
			curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_distance_title_both_records_global
	}
}

					market_goods_production > 200
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_power_line
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_scope_state = {
				is_coastal = yes
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_seagull
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_lightning
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_sabotage
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_updraft
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_livestock_ranch
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_stampede
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_failed_fixing
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_weak_spot
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_heart_attack
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_balloon_crash
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				has_strategic_land_adjacency = root
				has_technology_researched = military_aviation
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_fighter_intercepted
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_scope_state = {
				has_state_trait = state_trait_the_great_plains
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_tornado
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_fall
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_envelope_falls_apart
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				has_strategic_land_adjacency = root
				is_country_type = decentralized
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_killed_by_indigenous_people
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_cigar
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_scope_state = {
				OR = {
					has_state_trait = state_trait_alps_mountains
					has_state_trait = state_trait_pyrenees_mountains
					has_state_trait = state_trait_ural_mountains
					has_state_trait = state_trait_caucasus_mountains
					has_state_trait = state_trait_zagros_mountains
					has_state_trait = state_trait_zagros_mountains
					has_state_trait = state_trait_himalayas_mountains
					has_state_trait = state_trait_great_dividing_range
					has_state_trait = state_trait_scottish_highlands
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_killed_crash_mountainside
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_hail_storm
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
				has_trait = alcoholic
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_killed_alcohol
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
				has_trait = opium_addiction
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_killed_opium
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_acrobatics
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_goose
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_mile_high_club
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_scope_state = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_urban_center
					level >= 10
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_zoo_crocodile
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_cheap_parts
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_disappearance
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_scope_state = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_railway
					level >= 5
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_train
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_scope_state = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_skyscraper
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_skyscraper
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_disease
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_slipped
	}

	text = {
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_ladder
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
				has_ideology = ideology_market_liberal
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_angry_worker
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
				has_ideology = ideology:ideology_abolitionist
			}
			NOT = {
				has_law = law_type:law_slavery_banned
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_sabotage_slaver
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			exists = c:USA
			c:USA = root
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_death_shot_over_prison
	}
}



#Balloonist trait
curtiss_balloonist_trait_level_type = {
	type = country
	
	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_no_balloonist
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
				has_trait = curtiss_balloonist
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_balloonist
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
				has_trait = curtiss_balloonist_experienced
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_experienced_balloonist
	}

	text = {
		trigger = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
				has_trait = curtiss_balloonist_famous
			}
		}
		localization_key = curtiss_custom_famous_balloonist
	}
}
